### [79] [Can LLMs Beat Classical Hyperparameter Optimization Algorithms? A Study on autoresearch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24647)
*Fabio Ferreira,Lucca Wobbe,Arjun Krishnakumar,Frank Hutter,Arber Zela*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出autoresearch框架，对比LLM智能体与经典HPO算法在语言模型超参数优化上的表现。关键发现：1)无约束搜索空间中LLM能大幅缩小与经典方法的差距；2)避免内存失败比探索多样性更重要；3)提出的Centaur混合方法通过共享CMA-ES内部状态，使0.8B模型优于27B模型，达到最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典HPO方法缺乏领域知识，而LLM虽具备知识但难以跟踪优化状态。现有研究未充分探索LLM在无约束空间中的潜力及可靠性与探索性的平衡问题。

Method: 开发autoresearch库支持LLM直接编辑代码搜索超参数；在固定计算预算下，对比CMA-ES、TPE与LLM方法在固定/无约束空间的表现；提出Centaur混合框架，将CMA-ES的均值、步长、协方差矩阵共享给LLM。

Result: 固定空间中CMA-ES/TPE占优；无约束空间中LLM缩小差距；可靠性优于探索性；Centaur性能最佳；0.8B版本优于27B版本；0.8B虽无法独立编辑代码但足以支持混合优化。

Conclusion: 混合架构是超参数优化新方向；共享优化器状态可融合LLM领域知识与经典方法稳定性；小模型在混合框架中同样有效，降低成本；强调在资源约束下稳定性的重要性优于盲目探索。

Abstract: The autoresearch repository enables an LLM agent to search for optimal hyperparameter configurations on an unconstrained search space by editing the training code directly. Given a fixed compute budget and constraints, we use \emph{autoresearch} as a testbed to compare classical hyperparameter optimization (HPO) algorithms against LLM-based methods on tuning the hyperparameters of a small language model. Within a fixed hyperparameter search space, classical HPO methods such as CMA-ES and TPE consistently outperform LLM-based agents. However, an LLM agent that directly edits training source code in an unconstrained search space narrows the gap to classical methods substantially despite using only a self-hosted open-weight 27B model. Methods that avoid out-of-memory failures outperform those with higher search diversity, suggesting that reliability matters more than exploration breadth. While small and mid-sized LLMs struggle to track optimization state across trials, classical methods lack domain knowledge. To bridge this gap, we introduce Centaur, a hybrid that shares CMA-ES's internal state, including mean vector, step-size, and covariance matrix, with an LLM. Centaur achieves the best result in our experiments, with its 0.8B variant outperforming the 27B variant, suggesting that a cheap LLM suffices when paired with a strong classical optimizer. The 0.8B model is insufficient for unconstrained code editing but sufficient for hybrid optimization, while scaling to 27B provides no advantage for fixed search space methods with the open-weight models tested. Code is available at https://github.com/ferreirafabio/autoresearch-automl.

</details>


### [80] [Amplified Patch-Level Differential Privacy for Free via Random Cropping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24695)
*Kaan Durmaz,Jan Schuchardt,Sebastian Schmidt,Stephan Günnemann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了随机裁剪在差分隐私机器学习中的新作用。研究发现，随机裁剪能概率性地排除图像中的敏感局部内容（如人脸、车牌），从而引入第三种随机性来源，无需修改模型或训练过程即可增强隐私保护。通过引入patch级相邻关系和推导tight隐私边界，理论分析表明这种机制降低了有效采样率。实验验证了其在多个分割任务上改善了隐私-效用权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机裁剪是计算机视觉的常用数据增强技术，但其在差分隐私训练中的作用未被探索。现有DP-SGD的隐私保证依赖于梯度噪声和minibatch采样两种随机性，而随机裁剪可能通过排除敏感局部内容提供额外的隐私放大效果，这一现象亟待形式化分析和验证。

Method: 1) 提出视觉数据的patch级相邻关系来形式化随机裁剪的隐私效应；2) 推导DP-SGD结合随机裁剪的tight隐私边界；3) 量化patch包含概率及其对minibatch采样的复合作用；4) 在多个分割架构和数据集上进行实证验证。

Result: 理论分析表明随机裁剪通过patch排除引入第三种随机性，显著降低了有效采样率，实现了隐私放大。实证结果验证了在多种分割模型和benchmark数据集上，这种patch级隐私增强策略能在不增加成本的情况下改善隐私-效用权衡。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了随机裁剪在差分隐私训练中的隐藏价值，提供了一种无需额外开销的隐私增强机制。通过将隐私核算与领域结构对齐，研究为计算机视觉领域的隐私保护实践提供了新思路，证明了利用现有数据增强技术的随机性可以强化隐私保证。

Abstract: Random cropping is one of the most common data augmentation techniques in computer vision, yet the role of its inherent randomness in training differentially private machine learning models has thus far gone unexplored. We observe that when sensitive content in an image is spatially localized, such as a face or license plate, random cropping can probabilistically exclude that content from the model's input. This introduces a third source of stochasticity in differentially private training with stochastic gradient descent, in addition to gradient noise and minibatch sampling. This additional randomness amplifies differential privacy without requiring changes to model architecture or training procedure. We formalize this effect by introducing a patch-level neighboring relation for vision data and deriving tight privacy bounds for differentially private stochastic gradient descent (DP-SGD) when combined with random cropping. Our analysis quantifies the patch inclusion probability and shows how it composes with minibatch sampling to yield a lower effective sampling rate. Empirically, we validate that patch-level amplification improves the privacy-utility trade-off across multiple segmentation architectures and datasets. Our results demonstrate that aligning privacy accounting with domain structure and additional existing sources of randomness can yield stronger guarantees at no additional cost.

### [81] [Training LLMs for Multi-Step Tool Orchestration with Constrained Data Synthesis and Graduated Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24709)
*Cheng Jiayang,Xin Liu,Zhihan Zhang,Haoyang Wen,Zixuan Zhang,Qingyu Yin,Shiyang Li,Priyanka Nigam,Bing Yin,Chao Zhang,Yangqiu Song*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出双轨框架：1）构建基于大规模真实API响应缓存的强化学习环境，实现可控制复杂度的有效多步骤编排轨迹采样，生成效率远超无约束方法；2）设计分级奖励机制，将正确性分解为原子有效性（多粒度函数调用正确性）和编排正确性（工具排序与依赖关系处理）。

Result: 在ComplexFuncBench基准测试中，该方法在轮次准确率上取得显著提升。消融实验表明两个奖励组件不可或缺，单独使用任一组件都会导致性能大幅下降。

Conclusion: 该研究通过整合真实API数据与分级奖励设计，为多步骤工具编排提供了有效解决方案，证明了细粒度奖励信号在复杂工作流训练中的重要性。

Abstract: Multi-step tool orchestration, where LLMs must invoke multiple dependent APIs in the correct order while propagating intermediate outputs, remains challenging. State-of-the-art models frequently fail on full sequence execution, with parameter value errors accounting for a significant portion of failures. Training models to handle such workflows faces two obstacles: existing environments focus on simple per-turn function calls with simulated data, and binary rewards provide no signal for partial correctness.
  We present a framework addressing both challenges. First, we construct a reinforcement learning environment backed by a large-scale cache of real API responses, enabling a data synthesis pipeline that samples valid multi-step orchestration traces with controllable complexity and significantly higher generation efficiency than unconstrained methods. Second, we propose a graduated reward design that decomposes correctness into atomic validity (individual function call correctness at increasing granularity) and orchestration (correct tool sequencing with dependency respect). On ComplexFuncBench, our approach demonstrates substantial improvements in turn accuracy. Ablation studies confirm both reward components are essential: using either alone significantly degrades performance.

### [82] [Can an Actor-Critic Optimization Framework Improve Analog Design Optimization?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24714)
*Sounak Dutta,Fin Amin,Sushil Panda,Jonathan Rabe,Yuejiang Wen,Paul Franzon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种演员-评论家优化框架（ACOF）用于模拟电路尺寸设计。该框架通过分离搜索提议与评估角色，将设计师的判断力引入优化过程，使搜索更主动、稳定且可解释。在保持标准仿真流程兼容性的同时，ACOF在测试电路上平均提升前10名品质因数38.9%，降低遗憾度24.7%，单电路最高提升达70.5%的FoM和42.2%的遗憾度降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ACOF采用演员-评论家结构：演员负责推荐有前景的设计空间区域；评论家负责评估推荐、强制设计约束并在搜索受阻时重定向。该分离结构兼容标准仿真流程，使搜索过程更具目的性、稳定性和可解释性。

Result: 实验表明，相比最强竞争基线，ACOF平均提升前10名品质因数38.9%，平均降低遗憾度24.7%。在单个电路上，最高实现70.5%的FoM提升和42.2%的遗憾度降低。

Conclusion: 该框架通过结合迭代推理与仿真驱动搜索，为自动化模拟电路尺寸优化提供了更透明的路径，在保持标准流程兼容性的同时显著提升优化性能，适用于挑战性设计空间。

Abstract: Analog design often slows down because even small changes to device sizes or biases require expensive simulation cycles, and high-quality solutions typically occupy only a narrow part of a very large search space. While existing optimizers reduce some of this burden, they largely operate without the kind of judgment designers use when deciding where to search next. This paper presents an actor-critic optimization framework (ACOF) for analog sizing that brings that form of guidance into the loop. Rather than treating optimization as a purely black-box search problem, ACOF separates the roles of proposal and evaluation: an actor suggests promising regions of the design space, while a critic reviews those choices, enforces design legality, and redirects the search when progress is hampered. This structure preserves compatibility with standard simulator-based flows while making the search process more deliberate, stable, and interpretable. Across our test circuits, ACOF improves the top-10 figure of merit by an average of 38.9% over the strongest competing baseline and reduces regret by an average of 24.7%, with peak gains of 70.5% in FoM and 42.2% lower regret on individual circuits. By combining iterative reasoning with simulation-driven search, the framework offers a more transparent path toward automated analog sizing across challenging design spaces.

### [83] [GraphER: An Efficient Graph-Based Enrichment and Reranking Method for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24925)
*Ruizhong Miao,Yuying Wang,Rongguang Wang,Chenyang Li,Tao Sheng,Sujith Ravi,Dan Roth*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: GraphER采用两阶段方法：在离线索引阶段独立地对数据对象进行图增强，在查询时对候选对象执行基于图的重排序。该方法通过图结构捕捉语义相似性之外的多种邻近关系，无需构建知识图谱，可与标准向量存储无缝集成，且对检索器无依赖性，仅引入可忽略的延迟开销。

Result: 在多个检索基准测试上的实验结果表明，GraphER能有效提升检索性能，证明了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: GraphER成功克服了现有方法的局限性，提供了一种可与现有向量存储系统无缝集成的图增强重排序方案，为RAG系统中的复杂信息检索问题提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Semantic search in retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems is often insufficient for complex information needs, particularly when relevant evidence is scattered across multiple sources. Prior approaches to this problem include agentic retrieval strategies, which expand the semantic search space by generating additional queries. However, these methods do not fully leverage the organizational structure of the data and instead rely on iterative exploration, which can lead to inefficient retrieval. Another class of approaches employs knowledge graphs to model non-semantic relationships through graph edges. Although effective in capturing richer proximities, such methods incur significant maintenance costs and are often incompatible with the vector stores used in most production systems. To address these limitations, we propose GraphER, a graph-based enrichment and reranking method that captures multiple forms of proximity beyond semantic similarity. GraphER independently enriches data objects during offline indexing and performs graph-based reranking over candidate objects at query time. This design does not require a knowledge graph, allowing GraphER to integrate seamlessly with standard vector stores. In addition, GraphER is retriever-agnostic and introduces negligible latency overhead. Experiments on multiple retrieval benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach.

*Yuda Bi,Chenyu Zhang,Qiheng Wang,Vince D Calhoun*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Grokking -- the delayed onset of generalization after early memorization -- is often described with phase-transition language, but that claim has lacked falsifiable finite-size inputs. Here we supply those inputs by treating the group order $p$ of $\mathbb{Z}_p$ as an admissible extensive variable and a held-out spectral head-tail contrast as a representation-level order parameter, then apply a condensed-matter-style diagnostic chain to coarse-grid sweeps and a dense near-critical addition audit. Binder-like crossings reveal a shared finite-size boundary, and susceptibility comparison strongly disfavors a smooth-crossover interpretation ($Δ\mathrm{AIC}=16.8$ in the near-critical audit). Phase-transition language in grokking can therefore be tested as a quantitative finite-size claim rather than invoked as analogy alone, although the transition order remains unresolved at present.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准视觉模型将物体视为欧几里得空间中的独立点，无法捕捉部分与整体之间的层次结构。这种表示方式缺乏对物体内部组成部分关系的建模能力，限制了模型对复杂场景中层次化对象的理解。

Method: 提出Worldline Slot Attention方法，将每个物体建模为通过时空的持久轨迹（世界线）。每个物体在不同层次级别上拥有多个槽位，这些槽位共享相同的空间位置但在时间坐标上有所不同。该方法探索了不同几何结构（欧几里得、洛伦兹、双曲）下的世界线表示。

Result: 实验表明，缺乏几何结构时该架构会失败。欧几里得世界线仅达到0.078的层次准确率，低于随机猜测(0.33)。洛伦兹世界线在三个数据集上达到0.479-0.661的准确率，相比欧几里得方法提升6倍，且在20多次独立运行中得到复现。此外，洛伦兹几何优于双曲嵌入。

Conclusion: 视觉层次结构的发现需要能够编码非对称因果关系的时空几何结构，这种归纳偏置在欧几里得空间中缺失，但在洛伦兹光锥中自然存在。研究结果表明因果结构（时间依赖性）而非树状结构（径向分支）对视觉层次建模至关重要。该方法仅使用11K参数。

Abstract: Standard vision models treat objects as independent points in Euclidean space, unable to capture hierarchical structure like parts within wholes. We introduce Worldline Slot Attention, which models objects as persistent trajectories through spacetime worldlines, where each object has multiple slots at different hierarchy levels sharing the same spatial position but differing in temporal coordinates. This architecture consistently fails without geometric structure: Euclidean worldlines achieve 0.078 level accuracy, below random chance (0.33), while Lorentzian worldlines achieve 0.479-0.661 across three datasets: a 6x improvement replicated over 20+ independent runs. Lorentzian geometry also outperforms hyperbolic embeddings showing visual hierarchies require causal structure (temporal dependency) rather than tree structure (radial branching). Our results demonstrate that hierarchical object discovery requires geometric structure encoding asymmetric causality, an inductive bias absent from Euclidean space but natural to Lorentzian light cones, achieved with only 11K parameters. The code is available at: https://github.com/iclrsubmissiongram/loco.

</details>


### [86] [Transformers in the Dark: Navigating Unknown Search Spaces via Bandit Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24780)
*Jungtaek Kim,Thomas Zeng,Ziqian Lin,Minjae Lee,Chungpa Lee,Jy-yong Sohn,Hyung Il Koo,Kangwook Lee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管将大型语言模型与外部搜索算法结合能提升问题解决效果，但外部组件会复杂化整个过程。因此，论文提出核心问题：大型语言模型或其底层Transformer架构能否近似搜索算法？

Method: 作者引入了一个简化框架，其中树的扩展和反馈信号由外部指定，称为"未知树搜索与老虎机反馈"，以便可控地评估搜索能力。在此框架下，他们测试了Transformer实现不同搜索策略的理论表达能力，以及如何从零训练来近似这些策略，并通过在搜索轨迹上进行微调来解锁预训练语言模型的完整能力。

Result: 理论证明Transformer足够表达不同的搜索策略，且从零训练能够近似这些策略。Transformer模型展现出对未见条件（如更长视野或更深树结构）的泛化可能性。此外，通过在搜索轨迹上对预训练LLM进行任务导向的持续训练，可以解锁其全部能力。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型和Transformer架构确实能够近似搜索算法，而基于搜索轨迹的任务导向微调是释放其潜力的有效方法。

Abstract: Effective problem solving with Large Language Models (LLMs) can be enhanced when they are paired with external search algorithms. By viewing the space of diverse ideas and their follow-up possibilities as a tree structure, the search algorithm can navigate such a search space and guide the LLM toward better solutions more efficiently. While the search algorithm enables an effective balance between exploitation and exploration of a tree-structured space, the need for an external component can complicate the overall problem-solving process. We therefore pose the following question: Can LLMs or their underlying Transformer architectures approximate a search algorithm? To answer this question, we first introduce a simplified framework in which tree extensions and feedback signals are externally specified, allowing for controlled evaluation of search capabilities. We call this setting unknown tree search with bandit feedback. Within this setting, we show that Transformers are theoretically expressive enough to implement distinct search strategies and can be trained from scratch to approximate those strategies. Our Transformer models exhibit the possibility of generalizing to unseen conditions such as longer horizons or deeper trees. Furthermore, we demonstrate that continued task-focused training unlocks the complete capabilities of a pretrained LLM, by fine-tuning the LLM on search trajectories.

### [87] [A Practical Guide Towards Interpreting Time-Series Deep Clinical Predictive Models: A Reproducibility Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24828)

TL;DR: 该论文针对临床深度学习模型的可解释性问题开展系统性基准测试，发现注意力机制在正确使用时能高效准确地解释模型预测；而KernelSHAP和LIME等黑盒解释器在时间序列临床任务中计算不可行；且多种解释方法可靠性不足。研究提供了提升临床预测管道可解释性的指导原则，并通过开源框架PyHealth发布实现代码以促进可复现性。

Conclusion: 研究总结了提升临床预测管道可解释性的多项指导原则，并强调需开发更高效、可靠的解释方法。为实现可复现性和可扩展性，作者通过PyHealth开源框架公开代码（https://github.com/sunlabuiuc/PyHealth），为临床可信AI研究提供基础设施支持。

Abstract: Clinical decisions are high-stakes and require explicit justification, making model interpretability essential for auditing deep clinical models prior to deployment. As the ecosystem of model architectures and explainability methods expands, critical questions remain: Do architectural features like attention improve explainability? Do interpretability approaches generalize across clinical tasks? While prior benchmarking efforts exist, they often lack extensibility and reproducibility, and critically, fail to systematically examine how interpretability varies across the interplay of clinical tasks and model architectures. To address these gaps, we present a comprehensive benchmark evaluating interpretability methods across diverse clinical prediction tasks and model architectures. Our analysis reveals that: (1) attention when leveraged properly is a highly efficient approach for faithfully interpreting model predictions; (2) black-box interpreters like KernelSHAP and LIME are computationally infeasible for time-series clinical prediction tasks; and (3) several interpretability approaches are too unreliable to be trustworthy. From our findings, we discuss several guidelines on improving interpretability within clinical predictive pipelines. To support reproducibility and extensibility, we provide our implementations via PyHealth, a well-documented open-source framework: https://github.com/sunlabuiuc/PyHealth.

### [88] [Flow matching on homogeneous spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24829)
*Francesco Ruscelli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出齐性空间流匹配的通用框架，通过将数据分布提升到李群并进一步简化为李代数上的欧几里得流匹配，避免复杂几何计算，实现更简单、快速且内蕴的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将齐性空间问题提升为李群上的流匹配，利用李群-李代数对应简化为欧几里得流匹配，避免直接处理几何结构。

Result: 无需预度量和测地线计算，比黎曼流匹配更简单快速，同时保持完全内蕴性。

Conclusion: 通过李群-李代数桥梁成功扩展流匹配至齐性空间，为计算机视觉、机器人学等应用提供新方案。

Abstract: We propose a general framework to extend Flow Matching to homogeneous spaces, i.e. quotients of Lie groups. Our approach reformulates the problem as a flow matching task on the underlying Lie group by lifting the data distributions. This strategy avoids the potentially complicated geometry of homogeneous spaces by working directly on Lie groups, which in turn enables us reduce the problem to a Euclidean flow matching task on Lie algebras. In contrast to Riemannian Flow Matching, our method eliminates the need to define and compute premetrics or geodesics, resulting in a simpler, faster, and fully intrinsic framework.

### [89] [Reaching Beyond the Mode: RL for Distributional Reasoning in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24844)
*Isha Puri,Mehul Damani,Idan Shenfeld,Marzyeh Ghassemi,Jacob Andreas,Yoon Kim*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准语言模型后训练常将隐含答案分布坍缩至单一主导模式，这对医疗诊断、模糊问答等涉及多有效答案或不可约简不确定性的真实任务不适用。现有方法需计算密集型的重复采样来生成非模式化答案，效率低下。

Method: 提出多答案强化学习方法，修改RL目标函数，使模型在单次前向传播中显式生成多个候选答案，将推理时搜索过程内部化到生成过程中，实现分布推理。

Result: 在问答、医疗诊断和代码基准测试上，相比单答案训练基线，多样性、覆盖率和集合级校准分数显著提升。生成多答案所需token更少，代码任务准确率大幅提高。

Conclusion: 多答案RL是有原则且计算高效的替代方案，可替代best-of-k等推理时扩展过程，为处理多答案和不确定性任务提供了新训练范式。

Abstract: Given a question, a language model (LM) implicitly encodes a distribution over possible answers. In practice, post-training procedures for LMs often collapse this distribution onto a single dominant mode. While this is generally not a problem for benchmark-style evaluations that assume one correct answer, many real-world tasks inherently involve multiple valid answers or irreducible uncertainty. Examples include medical diagnosis, ambiguous question answering, and settings with incomplete information. In these cases, we would like LMs to generate multiple plausible hypotheses, ideally with confidence estimates for each one, and without computationally intensive repeated sampling to generate non-modal answers. This paper describes a multi-answer reinforcement learning approach for training LMs to perform distributional reasoning over multiple answers during inference. We modify the RL objective to enable models to explicitly generate multiple candidate answers in a single forward pass, internalizing aspects of inference-time search into the model's generative process. Across question-answering, medical diagnostic, and coding benchmarks, we observe improved diversity, coverage, and set-level calibration scores compared to single answer trained baselines. Models trained with our approach require fewer tokens to generate multiple answers than competing approaches. On coding tasks, they are also substantially more accurate. These results position multi-answer RL as a principled and compute-efficient alternative to inference-time scaling procedures such as best-of-k. Code and more information can be found at https://multi-answer-rl.github.io/.

Method: 研究在匹配仿真环境中开展对比实验：(1) 采用离线强化学习训练定制化Transformer策略，基于详细历史状态数据；(2) 探索大语言模型处理抽象化、人类可读状态描述，系统评估提示工程、自动提示优化、监督微调及直接偏好优化等策略。

Abstract: We investigate machine learning approaches for optimizing real-time staffing decisions in semi-automated warehouse sortation systems. Operational decision-making can be supported at different levels of abstraction, with different trade-offs. We evaluate two approaches, each in a matching simulation environment. First, we train custom Transformer-based policies using offline reinforcement learning on detailed historical state representations, achieving a 2.4% throughput improvement over historical baselines in learned simulators. In high-volume warehouse operations, improvements of this size translate to significant savings. Second, we explore LLMs operating on abstracted, human-readable state descriptions. These are a natural fit for decisions that warehouse managers make using high-level operational summaries. We systematically compare prompting techniques, automatic prompt optimization, and fine-tuning strategies. While prompting alone proves insufficient, supervised fine-tuning combined with Direct Preference Optimization on simulator-generated preferences achieves performance that matches or slightly exceeds historical baselines in a hand-crafted simulator. Our findings demonstrate that both approaches offer viable paths toward AI-assisted operational decision-making. Offline RL excels with task-specific architectures. LLMs support human-readable inputs and can be combined with an iterative feedback loop that can incorporate manager preferences.

*Haishan Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次为对抗环境下两点反馈在线凸优化中的μ-强凸损失提供了紧的高概率遗憾界O(d(log T + log(1/δ))/μ)，结果极小极大最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两点bandit反馈虽支持梯度估计，但估计器重尾特性阻碍了标准浓度分析，使强凸函数的高概率遗憾界成为自agarwal2010optimal以来的开放问题。

Method: 通过解决bandit梯度估计器的重尾分布挑战，开发新的高概率浓度分析工具，建立适用于强凸函数的遗憾界证明框架。

Conclusion: 该结果在T和d上均达到极小极大最优，完整解决了文献中的开放问题，奠定两点反馈在线凸优化的理论基础。

Abstract: We consider the problem of Online Convex Optimization (OCO) with two-point bandit feedback in an adversarial environment.
  In this setting, a player attempts to minimize a sequence of adversarially generated convex loss functions, while only observing the value of each function at two points.
  While it is well-known that two-point feedback allows for gradient estimation, achieving tight high-probability regret bounds for strongly convex functions still remained open as highlighted by \citet{agarwal2010optimal}. The primary challenge lies in the heavy-tailed nature of bandit gradient estimators, which makes standard concentration analysis difficult.
  In this paper, we resolve this open challenge by providing the first high-probability regret bound of $O(d(\log T + \log(1/δ))/μ)$ for $μ$-strongly convex losses. Our result is minimax optimal with respect to both the time horizon $T$ and the dimension $d$.

### [92] [Epistemic Compression: The Case for Deliberate Ignorance in High-Stakes AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25033)
*Steffen Lukas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 基础模型在稳定环境表现优异，但在医疗、金融、政策等高可靠性要求领域常失效。作者提出"保真度悖论"是结构性问题而非数据问题，引入"认知压缩"原则：鲁棒性源于模型复杂度与数据有效期的匹配，而非参数扩展。通过"体制指数"区分不稳定数据贫乏的"转移体制"与稳定数据丰富的"稳定体制"。对15个高风险领域的探索性综合显示86.7%的符合率，主张从盲目扩展转向原则性简约。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型等基础模型在稳定环境中表现出色，但在医疗、金融、政策等高风险、高可靠性要求领域却频繁失效。这种"保真度悖论"的根本原因不是数据不足，而是模型结构问题。在规则随时间变化的领域中，额外的模型容量会放大噪声而非捕获信号，导致模型在实际应用中不可靠。

Method: 提出"认知压缩"（Epistemic Compression）原则，通过在架构层面强制简约性来匹配模型复杂度与数据保质期。创新性地引入"体制指数"（Regime Index）区分两种建模情境：1）转移体制（Shifting Regime）：不稳定、数据贫乏，简约模型更优；2）稳定体制（Stable Regime）：不变、数据丰富，复杂模型可行。采用探索性综合分析，在15个高风险领域验证该指数的预测有效性。

Result: 对15个高风险领域的探索性综合分析显示，该体制指数与实证最优建模策略的符合率达到86.7%（13/15案例）。结果表明在数据有效期短、规则动态变化的领域，简约架构确实比盲目扩展参数更有效。

Conclusion: 高风险AI需要从单纯追求模型规模扩展，转向基于原则的简约性设计。认知压缩提供了一种新范式，通过架构层面的约束确保模型在动态环境中的鲁棒性和可靠性，而非依赖事后正则化或参数堆砌。

Abstract: Foundation models excel in stable environments, yet often fail where reliability matters most: medicine, finance, and policy. This Fidelity Paradox is not just a data problem; it is structural. In domains where rules change over time, extra model capacity amplifies noise rather than capturing signal. We introduce Epistemic Compression: the principle that robustness emerges from matching model complexity to the shelf life of the data, not from scaling parameters. Unlike classical regularization, which penalizes weights post hoc, Epistemic Compression enforces parsimony through architecture: the model structure itself is designed to reduce overfitting by making it architecturally costly to represent variance that exceeds the evidence in the data. We operationalize this with a Regime Index that separates Shifting Regime (unstable, data-poor; simplicity wins) from Stable Regime (invariant, data-rich; complexity viable). In an exploratory synthesis of 15 high-stakes domains, this index was concordant with the empirically superior modeling strategy in 86.7% of cases (13/15). High-stakes AI demands a shift from scaling for its own sake to principled parsimony.

</details>

### [94] [The Order Is The Message](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25047)
*Jordan LeDoux*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过模9973运算控制实验，仅改变训练示例顺序，发现两种特定排序策略能从仅占输入空间0.3%的数据中，分别在487和659个epoch实现99.5%测试准确率，远低于IID排序的样本复杂度下界；IID基线在5000个epoch后仅达0.30%准确率，对抗性排序则完全抑制学习。成功模型构建了傅里叶表示，其基频为排序结构的傅里叶对偶，编码了单个样本中不存在的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究训练数据排序对模型泛化的独立影响，挑战传统样本复杂度理论，理解非IID排序如何突破理论下界实现高效学习，并为"顿悟"现象提供新解释，同时评估其对AI安全审计的潜在风险。

Method: 在模9973算术任务上进行严格控制实验，固定所有超参数和数据集，仅系统性调整训练示例呈现顺序。对比分析两种固定排序策略、IID随机排序及对抗性排序的效果，采用测试准确率和傅里叶频谱分析作为核心评估手段，检验模型在不同随机种子和训练集构成下的鲁棒性。

Result: 特定排序策略在极少量数据下实现超高效学习（99.5%准确率，<700 epochs），显著优于IID基线（0.30%准确率，5000 epochs）。对抗性排序完全阻断学习。成功模型一致地构建傅里叶表示，其基频对应于排序结构的傅里叶对偶，该现象在不同随机种子和训练集构成下具有高度鲁棒性，证明模型学习到了排序本身的结构信息。

Conclusion: 数据排序是影响训练效率和泛化的关键因素，可突破理论样本复杂度下界。这挑战了对"顿悟"的传统理解，揭示其可能源于数据排序而非训练时长。同时发现了新的安全风险：利用排序结构可构建绕过内容级审计的信息通道，对AI安全治理具有重要警示意义。

Abstract: In a controlled experiment on modular arithmetic ($p = 9973$), varying only example ordering while holding all else constant, two fixed-ordering strategies achieve 99.5\% test accuracy by epochs 487 and 659 respectively from a training set comprising 0.3\% of the input space, well below established sample complexity lower bounds for this task under IID ordering. The IID baseline achieves 0.30\% after 5{,}000 epochs from identical data. An adversarially structured ordering suppresses learning entirely. The generalizing model reliably constructs a Fourier representation whose fundamental frequency is the Fourier dual of the ordering structure, encoding information present in no individual training example, with the same fundamental emerging across all seeds tested regardless of initialization or training set composition. We discuss implications for training efficiency, the reinterpretation of grokking, and the safety risks of a channel that evades all content-level auditing.

### [95] [SIGMA: Structure-Invariant Generative Molecular Alignment for Chemical Language Models via Autoregressive Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25062)
*Xinyu Wang,Fei Dou,Jinbo Bi,Minghu Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对线性化字符串表示导致的结构-序列多对一映射问题，提出SIGMA框架，通过token级对比学习对齐相同后缀的前缀潜在状态，并结合IsoBeam消除同构冗余，在保持序列生成效率的同时提升分子结构的保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性化字符串表示虽使自回归分子生成具备可扩展性，但存在根本性模态不匹配：单一分子图可映射到多个不同序列，导致"轨迹发散"问题——结构等价的子图因线性化历史不同而产生漂移的潜在表示，破坏了模型对分子对称性的识别，降低了生成效率和质量。

Method: 提出SIGMA框架，核心包括：(1) 结构不变生成分子对齐：通过token级对比学习目标，显式对齐共享相同后缀的前缀潜在状态，使模型严格识别几何对称性；(2) 同构束搜索(IsoBeam)：在推理阶段通过动态剪枝等价路径消除同构冗余。

Result: 在标准基准测试上，SIGMA有效弥合了序列可扩展性与图保真度之间的鸿沟，相比强基线模型展现出更优的样本效率和结构多样性。

Conclusion: SIGMA通过保持高效的字符串表示形式同时引入结构不变性约束，成功解决了线性化过程中的轨迹发散问题，为可扩展且保真的分子生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Linearized string representations serve as the foundation of scalable autoregressive molecular generation; however, they introduce a fundamental modality mismatch where a single molecular graph maps to multiple distinct sequences. This ambiguity leads to \textit{trajectory divergence}, where the latent representations of structurally equivalent partial graphs drift apart due to differences in linearization history. To resolve this without abandoning the efficient string formulation, we propose Structure-Invariant Generative Molecular Alignment (SIGMA). Rather than altering the linear representation, SIGMA enables the model to strictly recognize geometric symmetries via a token-level contrastive objective, which explicitly aligns the latent states of prefixes that share identical suffixes. Furthermore, we introduce Isomorphic Beam Search (IsoBeam) to eliminate isomorphic redundancy during inference by dynamically pruning equivalent paths. Empirical evaluations on standard benchmarks demonstrate that SIGMA bridges the gap between sequence scalability and graph fidelity, yielding superior sample efficiency and structural diversity in multi-parameter optimization compared to strong baselines.

</details>


### [96] [Gap Safe Screening Rules for Fast Training of Robust Support Vector Machines under Feature Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25221)
*Tan-Hau Nguyen,Thu-Le Tran,Kien Trung Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对鲁棒支持向量机(R-SVMs)训练复杂度高的问题，首次提出基于拉格朗日对偶的安全样本筛选规则，通过识别不确定性集合完全位于间隔两侧的样本安全缩减问题规模，在不影响最优解的前提下显著加速训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: R-SVMs通过最坏情况鲁棒优化处理特征噪声，虽提升可靠性却导致计算成本激增。现有安全筛选技术依赖Fenchel-Rockafellar对偶，无法适用于R-SVMs的非标准结构，亟需专门设计的筛选机制来突破计算瓶颈。

Method: 研究从拉格朗日对偶框架出发，先构建理想筛选规则，再借鉴GAP安全区域思想开发实用规则。核心是通过数学推导识别那些不确定性集合必定位于间隔超平面两侧的样本，在优化前将其安全剔除，从而缩小问题规模。

Result: 实验验证该方法能在保持原始分类准确率的同时，大幅降低R-SVMs的训练时间，证明了筛选规则的有效性和安全性。

Conclusion: 作为首个将安全筛选应用于最坏情况鲁棒监督学习的研究，本工作提出的拉格朗日对偶基筛选规则成功解决了R-SVMs的计算效率问题，为大规模鲁棒模型训练提供了新思路。

Abstract: Robust Support Vector Machines (R-SVMs) address feature noise by adopting a worst-case robust formulation that explicitly incorporates uncertainty sets into training. While this robustness improves reliability, it also leads to increased computational cost. In this work, we develop safe sample screening rules for R-SVMs that reduce the training complexity without affecting the optimal solution. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study to apply safe screening techniques to worst-case robust models in supervised machine learning. Our approach safely identifies training samples whose uncertainty sets are guaranteed to lie entirely on either side of the margin hyperplane, thereby reducing the problem size and accelerating optimization. Owing to the nonstandard structure of R-SVMs, the proposed screening rules are derived from the Lagrangian duality rather than the Fenchel-Rockafellar duality commonly used in recent methods. Based on this analysis, we first establish an ideal screening rule, and then derive a practical rule by adapting GAP-based safe regions to the robust setting. Experiments demonstrate that the proposed method significantly reduces training time while preserving classification accuracy.

</details>


### [97] [How Pruning Reshapes Features: Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Weight-Pruned Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25325)
*Hector Borobia,Elies Seguí-Mas,Guillermina Tormo-Carbó*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统性地探讨了非结构化权重剪枝如何重塑大语言模型的内部特征几何结构。通过使用稀疏自编码器(SAEs)作为可解释性探针，发现剪枝会优先破坏高频通用特征而保留低频稀有特征，表现出隐式特征选择的效果。其中Wanda剪枝方法比幅度剪枝能更好地保持特征结构，且几何特征存活率与因果重要性之间存在解离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 权重剪枝是大语言模型压缩的标准技术，但其对学习到的内部表示的影响尚不明确。本研究旨在填补这一空白，系统性地理解非结构化剪枝如何改变语言模型的特征几何结构，这对于模型压缩后的可解释性和性能理解具有重要意义。

Method: 研究采用稀疏自编码器(SAEs)作为可解释性探针，在三个模型家族(Gemma 3 1B、Gemma 2 2B、Llama 3.2 1B)、两种剪枝方法(幅度和Wanda)以及六个稀疏度水平(0-60%)上进行实验，探讨种子稳定性、特征存活、SAE可迁移性、特征脆弱性和因果相关性五个研究问题。

Result: 主要发现包括：(1)稀有特征(低激活率)比高频特征更能抵抗剪枝，在17个实验条件中有11个表现出-1.0的斯皮尔曼相关性；(2)Wanda剪枝比幅度剪枝能更好地保持特征结构，最高可达3.7倍；(3)预训练SAEs在Wanda剪枝模型上可达50%稀疏度仍保持有效性；(4)特征几何存活率不能预测因果重要性，存在解离现象。

Conclusion: 剪枝实际上起到了隐式特征选择的作用，优先保留专业化的稀有特征而非通用的常见特征。不同剪枝方法效果差异显著，Wanda明显优于幅度剪枝。研究揭示了压缩条件下可解释性的复杂性，特征几何存活与因果重要性之间的解离对模型压缩后的可解释性研究具有重要启示。

Abstract: Weight pruning is a standard technique for compressing large language models, yet its effect on learned internal representations remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic study of how unstructured pruning reshapes the feature geometry of language models, using Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) as interpretability probes. Across three model families (Gemma 3 1B, Gemma 2 2B, Llama 3.2 1B), two pruning methods (magnitude and Wanda), and six sparsity levels (0--60%), we investigate five research questions spanning seed stability, feature survival, SAE transferability, feature fragility, and causal relevance. Our most striking finding is that rare SAE features--those with low firing rates--survive pruning far better than frequent ones, with within-condition Spearman correlations of rho = -1.0 in 11 of 17 experimental conditions. This counter-intuitive result suggests that pruning acts as implicit feature selection, preferentially destroying high-frequency generic features while preserving specialized rare ones. We further show that Wanda pruning preserves feature structure up to 3.7x better than magnitude pruning, that pre-trained SAEs remain viable on Wanda-pruned models up to 50% sparsity, and that geometric feature survival does not predict causal importance--a dissociation with implications for interpretability under compression.

</details>


### [98] [From Intent to Evidence: A Categorical Approach for Structural Evaluation of Deep Research Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25342)
*Shuoling Liu,Zhiquan Tan,Kun Yi,Hui Wu,Yihan Li,Jiangpeng Yan,Liyuan Chen,Kai Chen,Qiang Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对深度研究智能体评估缺乏严谨基准的问题，提出了一种基于范畴论的理论框架，构建了包含296个问题的机制感知基准，从四个可解释维度对11个主流模型进行压力测试。评估结果显示SOTA模型平均准确率仅19.9%，揭示出现有智能体在多跳结构合成任务上的严重缺陷，尽管其在动态拓扑重排序和本体验证方面表现尚可，但仍依赖脆弱启发式而非系统性理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度研究智能体（DRAs）的评估主要依赖临时经验基准，这些启发式方法无法严格建模智能体行为，也不能充分测试长时程合成和歧义消解能力。这导致了对DRAs真实能力的认知偏差，无法识别其结构性缺陷。

Method: 通过范畴论视角形式化DRA行为，将深度研究工作流建模为保结构映射（函子）的组合。基于此理论框架，构建了一个包含296个问题的机制感知基准，从四个可解释轴面对智能体进行压力测试：顺序连接链遍历、V结构拉回交点验证、检索子结构的拓扑排序，以及通过Yoneda探针进行的本体证伪。

Result: 对11个领先模型的严格评估建立了极低基线，SOTA模型平均准确率仅为19.9%。研究发现显著的能力二分法：先进深度研究管道在动态拓扑重排序和本体验证方面表现稳健，甚至能与纯推理模型匹敌，但在多跳结构合成任务上几乎完全崩溃。性能在不同任务间存在巨大差异，暴露出对脆弱启发式的持续依赖。

Conclusion: 尽管顶级自主智能体现在能够有机地统一搜索与推理，在动态拓扑重排序和本体验证方面取得进展，但实现对复杂结构信息的通用掌握仍是一个严峻的开放挑战。评估揭示出现有系统缺乏系统性理解，依赖启发式方法而非真正的结构推理能力。

Abstract: Although deep research agents (DRAs) have emerged as a promising paradigm for complex information synthesis, their evaluation remains constrained by ad hoc empirical benchmarks. These heuristic approaches do not rigorously model agent behavior or adequately stress-test long-horizon synthesis and ambiguity resolution. To bridge this gap, we formalize DRA behavior through the lens of category theory, modeling deep research workflow as a composition of structure-preserving maps (functors). Grounded in this theoretical framework, we introduce a novel mechanism-aware benchmark with 296 questions designed to stress-test agents along four interpretable axes: traversing sequential connectivity chains, verifying intersections within V-structure pullbacks, imposing topological ordering on retrieved substructures, and performing ontological falsification via the Yoneda Probe. Our rigorous evaluation of 11 leading models establishes a persistently low baseline, with the state-of-the-art achieving only a 19.9\% average accuracy, exposing the difficulty of formal structural stress-testing. Furthermore, our findings reveal a stark dichotomy in the current AI capabilities. While advanced deep research pipelines successfully redefine dynamic topological re-ordering and exhibit robust ontological verification -- matching pure reasoning models in falsifying hallucinated premises -- they almost universally collapse on multi-hop structural synthesis. Crucially, massive performance variance across tasks exposes a lingering reliance on brittle heuristics rather than a systemic understanding. Ultimately, this work demonstrates that while top-tier autonomous agents can now organically unify search and reasoning, achieving a generalized mastery over complex structural information remains a formidable open challenge.\footnote{Our implementation will be available at https://github.com/tzq1999/CDR.

</details>


### [99] [Hessian-informed machine learning interatomic potential towards bridging theory and experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25373)
*Bangchen Yin,Jian Ouyang,Zhen Fan,Kailai Lin,Hanshi Hu,Dingshun Lv,Weiluo Ren,Hai Xiao,Ji Chen,Changsu Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Hessian信息的机器学习原子间势（Hi-MLIP）及其高效训练策略HINT，通过大幅减少对昂贵Hessian标签的需求，实现了对势能面局部曲率的准确捕捉，显著提升了过渡态搜索和吉布斯自由能预测精度，并能有效处理强非谐体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 势能面的局部曲率对于从第一性原理预测分子和材料的实验观测量至关重要，但对于复杂体系而言仍难以企及。现有机器学习原子间势在曲率感知方面存在局限，而直接监督Hessian矩阵计算成本过高。

Method: 提出Hi-MLIP框架和HINT训练协议，通过Hessian预训练、构型采样、课程学习和随机投影Hessian损失等关键技术，以2-4个数量级的效率提升减少对Hessian标签的需求。

Result: Hi-MLIP显著改善了过渡态搜索精度，在数据稀缺情况下使吉布斯自由能预测接近化学精度；对强非谐氢化物体系能准确再现声子重整化和超导临界温度，结果与实验高度吻合，同时避免了非谐计算的昂贵计算瓶颈。

Conclusion: 该工作为增强机器学习原子间势的曲率感知能力提供了实用路径，有效连接了模拟计算与实验观测量，在多种体系中展现了良好的应用前景。

Abstract: Local curvature of potential energy surfaces is critical for predicting certain experimental observables of molecules and materials from first principles, yet it remains far beyond reach for complex systems. In this work, we introduce a Hessian-informed Machine Learning Interatomic Potential (Hi-MLIP) that captures such curvature reliably, thereby enabling accurate analysis of associated thermodynamic and kinetic phenomena. To make Hessian supervision practically viable, we develop a highly efficient training protocol, termed Hessian INformed Training (HINT), achieving two to four orders of magnitude reduction for the requirement of expensive Hessian labels. HINT integrates critical techniques, including Hessian pre-training, configuration sampling, curriculum learning and stochastic projection Hessian loss. Enabled by HINT, Hi-MLIP significantly improves transition-state search and brings Gibbs free-energy predictions close to chemical accuracy especially in data-scarce regimes. Our framework also enables accurate treatment of strongly anharmonic hydrides, reproducing phonon renormalization and superconducting critical temperatures in close agreement with experiment while bypassing the computational bottleneck of anharmonic calculations. These results establish a practical route to enhancing curvature awareness of machine learning interatomic potentials, bridging simulation and experimental observables across a wide range of systems.

### [100] [GlowQ: Group-Shared LOw-Rank Approximation for Quantized LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25385)
*Selim An,Il hong Suh,Yeseong Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对低比特量化导致的大语言模型精度下降问题，现有低秩修正方法虽能缓解但会引入高延迟和内存开销。为此，本文提出GlowQ及其选择性变体GlowQ-S，通过组共享的低秩近似和缓存复用机制，仅对收益最高的组或层进行修正。实验表明，GlowQ在降低5.6%首token延迟的同时提升9.6%吞吐量，并改善困惑度和下游任务精度；GlowQ-S进一步优化，可降低23.4%延迟并提升37.4%吞吐量，同时保持精度损失在0.2个百分点以内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低比特量化技术（如BitsAndBytes、AWQ、GPTQ）在部署大语言模型时会导致精度显著下降。虽然低秩修正方法（如LQER、QERA、ASER）能够缓解这一问题，但它们需要在所有层中插入误差校正模块，导致延迟和内存开销增加，限制了其在资源受限场景下的实用性。

Method: 提出GlowQ（Group-shared Low-rank approximation for quantized LLMs），核心思想是：1）按输入共享组对模型层进行分组；2）每组仅缓存一个共享的右因子矩阵；3）计算每组的高精度投影并跨模块复用；4）仅对精度收益最高的组或层应用校正。进一步提出选择性变体GlowQ-S，仅在收益最大的位置应用缓存模块，实现更细粒度的开销控制。

Result: 在WikiText-2等基准测试上，与强基线相比：GlowQ平均降低首token延迟5.6%，提升吞吐量9.6%，困惑度降低0.17%，下游任务精度提升0.42个百分点；GlowQ-S进一步将延迟降低23.4%，吞吐量提升37.4%，同时精度损失控制在平均0.2个百分点以内。

Conclusion: GlowQ通过组共享的低秩近似机制，在保持层特定校正表达力的同时显著降低了参数和内存开销。GlowQ-S的选择性策略进一步实现了延迟与吞吐量的大幅优化，为低比特量化大语言模型的部署提供了高效实用的解决方案，在资源效率与模型精度之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: Quantization techniques such as BitsAndBytes, AWQ, and GPTQ are widely used as a standard method in deploying large language models but often degrades accuracy when using low-bit representations, e.g., 4 bits. Low-rank correction methods (e.g., LQER, QERA, ASER) has been proposed to mitigate this issue, however, they restore all layers and insert error-correction modules into every decoder block, which increases latency and memory overhead. To address this limitation, we propose GlowQ, a group-shared low-rank approximation for quantized LLMs that caches a single shared right factor per input-sharing group and restores only the groups or layers that yield the highest accuracy benefit. GlowQ computes the high-precision projection once per input-sharing group and reuses it across its modules, reducing parameter and memory overhead, and retaining the expressivity of layer-specific corrections. We also propose a selective variant, GlowQ-S, that applies the cached shared module only where it provides the largest benefit. Compared with strong baselines, our approach reduces TTFB by (5.6%) and increases throughput by (9.6%) on average, while reducing perplexity on WikiText-2 by (0.17%) and increasing downstream accuracy by 0.42 percentage points. The selective model GlowQ-S further reduces latency, cutting TTFB by (23.4%) and increasing throughput by (37.4%), while maintaining accuracy within 0.2 percentage points on average.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零样本RL的下游性能高度依赖预训练数据质量，但无先验知识下收集相关多样数据集仍是挑战。现有无向探索导致数据多样性低，策略性能差且不适用于实际硬件部署。

Method: 在Forward-Backward算法基础上，提出FB-MEBE：1) 采用无监督行为探索策略，通过最大化已实现行为分布的熵来促进探索；2) 引入正则化评论家，将恢复的策略塑造成更自然、物理合理的行。

Conclusion: FB-MEBE通过熵最大化探索和正则化批评，有效解决了零样本RL中数据多样性不足和策略不实用的问题，为真实机器人控制提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms aim to learn a family of policies from a reward-free dataset, and recover optimal policies for any reward function directly at test time. Naturally, the quality of the pretraining dataset determines the performance of the recovered policies across tasks. However, pre-collecting a relevant, diverse dataset without prior knowledge of the downstream tasks of interest remains a challenge. In this work, we study $\textit{online}$ zero-shot RL for quadrupedal control on real robotic systems, building upon the Forward-Backward (FB) algorithm. We observe that undirected exploration yields low-diversity data, leading to poor downstream performance and rendering policies impractical for direct hardware deployment. Therefore, we introduce FB-MEBE, an online zero-shot RL algorithm that combines an unsupervised behavior exploration strategy with a regularization critic. FB-MEBE promotes exploration by maximizing the entropy of the achieved behavior distribution. Additionally, a regularization critic shapes the recovered policies toward more natural and physically plausible behaviors. We empirically demonstrate that FB-MEBE achieves and improved performance compared to other exploration strategies in a range of simulated downstream tasks, and that it renders natural policies that can be seamlessly deployed to hardware without further finetuning. Videos and code available on our website.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解多元时间序列中的有向时序交互对于解析复杂动力系统及预测模型至关重要。然而，现有方法多聚焦于从数据生成过程推断因果结构，缺乏对固定预训练预测器如何依赖历史输入进行预测的模型隐含结构解释能力。

Method: 提出Causal-INSIGHT框架，在推理时对输入施加系统性干预式钳制，根据预训练预测器的响应构建有向时序影响信号。同时提出Qbic准则，一种稀疏感知的图选择标准，可在无需真实图标签的情况下平衡预测保真度与结构复杂度。

Result: 在合成、模拟和真实基准测试上的实验表明，Causal-INSIGHT能够泛化到不同骨干架构，保持结构准确性竞争力，并在应用于现有预测器时显著改进时滞定位效果。

Conclusion: Causal-INSIGHT框架有效解决了模型隐含时序依赖结构的解释问题，为理解复杂动态系统中的预测机制提供了有力的分析工具，具有广泛的适用性和实用价值。

Abstract: Understanding directed temporal interactions in multivariate time series is essential for interpreting complex dynamical systems and the predictive models trained on them. We present Causal-INSIGHT, a model-agnostic, post-hoc interpretation framework for extracting model-implied (predictor-dependent), directed, time-lagged influence structure from trained temporal predictors. Rather than inferring causal structure at the level of the data-generating process, Causal-INSIGHT analyzes how a fixed, pre-trained predictor responds to systematic, intervention-inspired input clamping applied at inference time.
  From these responses, we construct directed temporal influence signals that reflect the dependencies the predictor relies on for prediction, and introduce Qbic, a sparsity-aware graph selection criterion that balances predictive fidelity and structural complexity without requiring ground-truth graph labels. Experiments across synthetic, simulated, and realistic benchmarks show that Causal-INSIGHT generalizes across diverse backbone architectures, maintains competitive structural accuracy, and yields significant improvements in temporal delay localization when applied to existing predictors.

### [106] [Revisiting On-Policy Distillation: Empirical Failure Modes and Simple Fixes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25562)
*Yuqian Fu,Haohuan Huang,Kaiwen Jiang,Yuanheng Zhu,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对大语言模型在长时序任务中在线策略蒸馏（OPD）的采样token变体脆弱性问题，从理论和实现两个层面重新审视OPD。理论分析表明token级OPD相对于序列级反向KL存在偏差但方差界更紧，实证研究识别出三种失败模式（不平衡的单token信号、学生生成前缀的不可靠教师指导、分词器或特殊token失配），并提出教师top-K局部支持匹配方法，在数学推理和智能体多任务训练中实现更稳定的优化和更优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线策略蒸馏（OPD）因评估学生生成轨迹而非固定教师轨迹而具有吸引力，但在长时序任务中，常用的采样token变体存在脆弱性：它将分布匹配简化为单token信号，且随着轨迹偏离教师常见前缀而变得不可靠。这促使作者从估计器和实现角度重新审视OPD的缺陷根源，以开发更稳定的训练目标。

Method: 研究采用理论与实证相结合的方法：首先从理论上分析token级OPD的偏差-方差权衡特性，通过玩具实验验证未来奖励耦合强度对梯度方差的影响；然后识别采样token OPD的三种失败模式（单token信号不平衡、学生前缀的教师指导不可靠、tokenizer/特殊token失配）；最终提出教师top-K局部支持匹配方案，结合截断反向KL、top-p轨迹采样和特殊token掩码进行实现。

Result: 在单任务数学推理和多任务智能体加数学训练中，所提方法相比采样token OPD实现了更稳定的优化过程和更好的下游性能。实证结果验证了token级OPD的偏差-方差权衡：更强的未来奖励耦合导致更高的梯度方差和更不稳定的学习。

Conclusion: 采样token OPD在长时序任务中的脆弱性源于其理论缺陷和实现局限，通过教师top-K局部支持匹配的截断反向KL目标可以有效缓解。该方法平衡了估计偏差与方差，解决了单token信号不平衡、教师指导不可靠及tokenizer失配问题，为大语言模型后训练提供了更稳定的蒸馏范式。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) is appealing for large language model (LLM) post-training because it evaluates teacher feedback on student-generated rollouts rather than fixed teacher traces. In long-horizon settings, however, the common sampled-token variant is fragile: it reduces distribution matching to a one-token signal and becomes increasingly unreliable as rollouts drift away from prefixes the teacher commonly visits. We revisit OPD from the estimator and implementation sides. Theoretically, token-level OPD is biased relative to sequence-level reverse-KL, but it has a much tighter worst-case variance bound; our toy study shows the same tradeoff empirically, with stronger future-reward coupling producing higher gradient variance and less stable learning. Empirically, we identify three failure modes of sampled-token OPD: an imbalanced one-token signal, unreliable teacher guidance on student-generated prefixes, and distortions caused by tokenizer or special-token mismatch. We address these issues with teacher top-K local support matching, implemented as truncated reverse-KL with top-p rollout sampling and special-token masking. Across single-task math reasoning and multi-task agentic-plus-math training, this objective yields more stable optimization and better downstream performance than sampled-token OPD.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经缩放定律已在自然语言处理和计算机视觉领域成为构建基础模型的基石，但在科学机器学习领域（特别是天气预报）尚未被系统研究。本研究旨在将缩放定律应用于科学领域，探索天气预报模型的缩放行为，以指导高效模型训练和资源分配。

Method: 研究采用极简、可扩展的Swin Transformer架构作为基础模型，使用持续训练策略，包括恒定学习率和周期性冷却阶段。通过系统探索不同模型大小、数据集规模和计算预算，构建了IsoFLOP曲线来分析缩放行为，并识别计算最优的训练配置。

Result: 研究发现，采用该极简训练方式的模型表现出可预测的缩放趋势，且优于标准的余弦学习率调度。冷却阶段可被重新用于提升下游性能，如实现更长时间跨度的多步预测滚动，以及通过频谱损失调整获得更精确的预测。研究还确定了不同计算预算下的最优训练方案。

Conclusion: 研究证明神经缩放定律可作为科学机器学习领域高效资源分配的重要诊断工具，外推缩放趋势可揭示潜在性能极限。这为未来大规模天气模型的开发提供了理论指导和最佳实践，同时开源代码确保了研究的可复现性。

Abstract: Neural scaling laws, which in some domains can predict the performance of large neural networks as a function of model, data, and compute scale, are the cornerstone of building foundation models in Natural Language Processing and Computer Vision. We study neural scaling in Scientific Machine Learning, focusing on models for weather forecasting. To analyze scaling behavior in as simple a setting as possible, we adopt a minimal, scalable, general-purpose Swin Transformer architecture, and we use continual training with constant learning rates and periodic cooldowns as an efficient training strategy. We show that models trained in this minimalist way follow predictable scaling trends and even outperform standard cosine learning rate schedules. Cooldown phases can be re-purposed to improve downstream performance, e.g., enabling accurate multi-step rollouts over longer forecast horizons as well as sharper predictions through spectral loss adjustments. We also systematically explore a wide range of model and dataset sizes under various compute budgets to construct IsoFLOP curves, and we identify compute-optimal training regimes. Extrapolating these trends to larger scales highlights potential performance limits, demonstrating that neural scaling can serve as an important diagnostic for efficient resource allocation. We open-source our code for reproducibility.

</details>


### [108] [A Unified Memory Perspective for Probabilistic Trustworthy AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25692)
*Xueji Zhao,Likai Pei,Jianbo Liu,Kai Ni,Ningyuan Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了统一的数据访问视角，将确定性访问视为随机采样的极限情况，以此分析可信AI的概率计算负载。基于此视角，定义了内存级评估标准，分析了传统架构的局限性，并探讨了概率计算内存架构的发展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可信人工智能越来越依赖概率计算来实现鲁棒性、可解释性、安全性和隐私性。在实际系统中，这类工作负载将确定性数据访问与跨模型、数据路径和系统函数的重复随机采样交织在一起，导致性能瓶颈从算术单元转移到必须同时提供数据和随机性的内存系统。

Method: 提出统一的数据访问视角，将确定性访问视为随机采样的极限情况，在通用框架内分析两种模式。基于此洞察，定义内存级评估标准，分析传统架构局限，并考察新兴的概率计算内存方法。

Result: 揭示增加随机需求会降低有效数据访问效率，并可能使系统进入熵限制运行状态。提出了包括统一操作、分布可编程性、效率、硬件非理想性鲁棒性和并行兼容性在内的内存级评估标准。

Conclusion: 通过分析传统架构的局限性和考察概率计算内存方法，为可扩展的可信AI硬件发展路径提供了方向。

Abstract: Trustworthy artificial intelligence increasingly relies on probabilistic computation to achieve robustness, interpretability, security and privacy. In practical systems, such workloads interleave deterministic data access with repeated stochastic sampling across models, data paths and system functions, shifting performance bottlenecks from arithmetic units to memory systems that must deliver both data and randomness. Here we present a unified data-access perspective in which deterministic access is treated as a limiting case of stochastic sampling, enabling both modes to be analyzed within a common framework. This view reveals that increasing stochastic demand reduces effective data-access efficiency and can drive systems into entropy-limited operation. Based on this insight, we define memory-level evaluation criteria, including unified operation, distribution programmability, efficiency, robustness to hardware non-idealities and parallel compatibility. Using these criteria, we analyze limitations of conventional architectures and examine emerging probabilistic compute-in-memory approaches that integrate sampling with memory access, outlining pathways toward scalable hardware for trustworthy AI.

</details>

### [109] [Pseudo Label NCF for Sparse OHC Recommendation: Dual Representation Learning and the Separability Accuracy Trade off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24750)
*Pronob Kumar Barman,Tera L. Reynolds. James Foulds*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对在线健康社区中因交互极度稀疏导致的个性化推荐难题，本研究提出伪标签神经协同过滤模型，通过融合用户16维问卷向量与群组特征，在冷启动条件下显著提升推荐性能（HR@5提升1-2倍），同时生成可解释的语义对齐嵌入空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线健康社区中，新用户在缺乏历史交互数据时面临支持群组发现的挑战。传统协同过滤方法在极端稀疏交互场景下效果不佳，亟需利用问卷等辅助信息构建可解释且有效的推荐系统。

Method: 扩展神经协同过滤架构（包括矩阵分解、多层感知机和NeuMF），引入基于问卷特征与群组特征余弦相似度的伪标签辅助学习目标。模型学习双重嵌入空间：主任务嵌入空间用于排名，伪标签嵌入空间用于语义对齐。

Result: 在165名用户和498个支持群组的冷启动数据集上，伪标签变体均提升排名性能：MLP的HR@5从2.65%提升至5.30%，NeuMF从4.46%提升至5.18%，MF从4.58%提升至5.42%。嵌入空间的可分性显著提高（轮廓系数提升），但存在可解释性与性能之间的权衡。

Conclusion: 问卷衍生的伪标签有效缓解了极端稀疏性下的推荐问题，在提升推荐准确性的同时产生了可解释的任务特定嵌入空间，为冷启动推荐提供了新思路。

Abstract: Online Health Communities connect patients for peer support, but users face a discovery challenge when they have minimal prior interactions to guide personalization. We study recommendation under extreme interaction sparsity in a survey driven setting where each user provides a 16 dimensional intake vector and each support group has a structured feature profile. We extend Neural Collaborative Filtering architectures, including Matrix Factorization, Multi Layer Perceptron, and NeuMF, with an auxiliary pseudo label objective derived from survey group feature alignment using cosine similarity mapped to [0, 1]. The resulting Pseudo Label NCF learns dual embedding spaces: main embeddings for ranking and pseudo label embeddings for semantic alignment.
  We evaluate on a dataset of 165 users and 498 support groups using a leave one out protocol that reflects cold start conditions. All pseudo label variants improve ranking performance: MLP improves HR@5 from 2.65% to 5.30%, NeuMF from 4.46% to 5.18%, and MF from 4.58% to 5.42%. Pseudo label embedding spaces also show higher cosine silhouette scores than baseline embeddings, with MF improving from 0.0394 to 0.0684 and NeuMF from 0.0263 to 0.0653. We further observe a negative correlation between embedding separability and ranking accuracy, indicating a trade off between interpretability and performance.
  These results show that survey derived pseudo labels improve recommendation under extreme sparsity while producing interpretable task specific embedding spaces.

</details>


### [110] [DIET: Learning to Distill Dataset Continually for Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24958)
*Jiaqing Zhang,Hao Wang,Mingjia Yin,Bo Chen,Qinglin Jia,Rui Zhou,Ruiming Tang,ChaoYi Ma,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出DIET框架以解决推荐系统全量数据重训成本高昂的问题。该框架通过流式数据集蒸馏，将演化数据流压缩为1-2%大小的动态蒸馏集，在双层优化框架下基于影响力感知机制进行阶段式更新，在保持与全量数据一致性能趋势的同时，实现高达60倍的迭代加速，且蒸馏数据具备跨架构泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模推荐系统采用持续学习范式处理海量流式行为日志，但全量历史数据重训在架构比较与迭代中成本过高，严重制约模型开发效率。现有静态数据集蒸馏方法无法适应数据流的动态演化，亟需能够持续维护蒸馏数据、忠实反映全量训练行为的流式蒸馏方案。

Method: DIET框架将蒸馏数据视为演化的训练记忆，采用阶段式更新策略以对齐长期训练动态。在双层优化框架下，首先基于影响力样本进行原则性初始化，随后通过影响力感知的记忆寻址机制实现选择性更新，从而在紧凑数据集上保留关键的训练信号。

Result: 实验表明，DIET可将训练数据压缩至原大小的1-2%，性能趋势与全量数据训练高度一致，模型迭代成本降低达60倍。此外，所生成的蒸馏数据集在不同模型架构间展现出良好的泛化性能，验证了其作为可扩展数据基础的有效性。

Conclusion: 流式数据集蒸馏为推荐系统开发提供了可扩展且可重用的数据基础，能够显著降低模型迭代成本，加速架构搜索与优化过程，是构建高效推荐系统训练基础设施的重要方向。

Abstract: Modern deep recommender models are trained under a continual learning paradigm, relying on massive and continuously growing streaming behavioral logs. In large-scale platforms, retraining models on full historical data for architecture comparison or iteration is prohibitively expensive, severely slowing down model development. This challenge calls for data-efficient approaches that can faithfully approximate full-data training behavior without repeatedly processing the entire evolving data stream. We formulate this problem as \emph{streaming dataset distillation for recommender systems} and propose \textbf{DIET}, a unified framework that maintains a compact distilled dataset which evolves alongside streaming data while preserving training-critical signals. Unlike existing dataset distillation methods that construct a static distilled set, DIET models distilled data as an evolving training memory and updates it in a stage-wise manner to remain aligned with long-term training dynamics. DIET enables effective continual distillation through principled initialization from influential samples and selective updates guided by influence-aware memory addressing within a bi-level optimization framework. Experiments on large-scale recommendation benchmarks demonstrate that DIET compresses training data to as little as \textbf{1-2\%} of the original size while preserving performance trends consistent with full-data training, reducing model iteration cost by up to \textbf{60$\times$}. Moreover, the distilled datasets produced by DIET generalize well across different model architectures, highlighting streaming dataset distillation as a scalable and reusable data foundation for recommender system development.

</details>


### [111] [Unbiased Multimodal Reranking for Long-Tail Short-Video Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24975)
*Wenyi Xu,Feiran Zhu,Songyang Li,Renzhe Zhou,Chao Zhang,Chenglei Dai,Yuren Mao,Yunjun Gao,Yi Zhang*

TL;DR: 快手面临长尾查询的马太效应问题，稀疏用户行为数据导致模型放大低质内容。本文提出LLM驱动的多模态重排序框架，通过两阶段训练（监督微调+偏好优化）估计用户体验，使用LLM的世界知识评估内容质量，不依赖用户行为。实验证明该方法在离线指标和在线A/B测试中均显著提升长尾视频搜索质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快手每日处理数亿次搜索，但长尾查询存在严重马太效应：由于用户行为数据稀疏，模型会放大点击诱饵和浅层内容等低质视频。传统方法依赖用户交互数据，在长尾场景下效果不佳。因此需要利用LLM的内在世界知识来评估内容质量，减少对稀疏用户行为的依赖。

Method: 提出LLM驱动的多模态重排序框架，包含两阶段训练过程：
1. 第一阶段：利用多模态证据构建高质量标注数据，进行监督微调
2. 第二阶段：引入成对偏好优化，使模型学习候选视频间的偏序关系
推理时，生成的体验分数用于提升高质量但曝光不足的视频，并通过强化学习指导页面级优化。

Result: - 离线实验：在AUC、NDCG@K和人工偏好判断等指标上持续优于强基线
- 在线A/B测试：覆盖15%流量，在用户体验和消费指标上均取得显著提升
证明了该方法在长尾视频搜索场景中的实际价值。

Conclusion: 利用LLM的世界知识进行内容质量评估是解决长尾查询马太效应的有效方案。该框架无需实时用户行为，通过两阶段训练和多模态信息，显著提升了搜索结果质量和用户体验，为视频搜索系统的优化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Kuaishou serving hundreds of millions of searches daily, the quality of short-video search is paramount. However, it suffers from a severe Matthew effect on long-tail queries: sparse user behavior data causes models to amplify low-quality content such as clickbait and shallow content. The recent advancements in Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a new paradigm, as their inherent world knowledge provides a powerful mechanism to assess content quality, agnostic to sparse user interactions. To this end, we propose a LLM-driven multimodal reranking framework, which estimates user experience without real user behavior. The approach involves a two-stage training process: the first stage uses multimodal evidence to construct high-quality annotations for supervised fine-tuning, while the second stage incorporates pairwise preference optimization to help the model learn partial orderings among candidates. At inference time, the resulting experience scores are used to promote high-quality but underexposed videos in reranking, and further guide page-level optimization through reinforcement learning. Experiments show that the proposed method achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines in offline metrics including AUC, NDCG@K, and human preference judgement. An online A/B test covering 15\% of traffic further demonstrates gains in both user experience and consumption metrics, confirming the practical value of the approach in long-tail video search scenarios.

### [112] [Sparton: Fast and Memory-Efficient Triton Kernel for Learned Sparse Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25011)
*Thong Nguyen,Cosimo Rulli,Franco Maria Nardini,Rossano Venturini,Andrew Yates*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对学习稀疏检索模型中的词汇表内存瓶颈问题，提出Sparton——一种基于Triton的融合GPU内核，通过瓦片矩阵乘法和早期在线规约避免全逻辑矩阵的物化，在30k-250k词表规模下实现最高4.8倍加速和数量级内存降低，使训练批次大小提升26倍的同时保持效果无损。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前最优的LSR模型（如Splade）采用LM头将隐藏状态投影到词汇锚定的逻辑矩阵，但30,000至250,000+的词表规模导致巨大的内存瓶颈和算子间I/O开销，严重限制了模型扩展和训练吞吐。传统元素级操作和池化流程必须物化完整逻辑矩阵，造成不必要的内存占用和性能瓶颈。

Method: 设计Sparton Triton内核，将瓦片矩阵乘法、ReLU激活、Log1P变换和序列维度的最大规约操作融合为单一GPU内核。核心创新在于对原始逻辑瓦片执行早期在线规约，在计算过程中直接聚合稀疏表示，从而完全避免全尺寸逻辑矩阵的内存物化。

Result: 独立内核测试显示，相比PyTorch基线实现最高4.8倍速度提升，内存峰值使用量降低一个数量级。集成至Splade（|V|≈30k）后，批次大小扩大33%，训练速度提升14%且检索效果无损失；在词表规模250k的多语言模型上，批次大小扩大26倍，训练速度提升2.5倍。

Conclusion: Sparton通过算子融合和在线规约策略有效消除了LSR模型的内存墙问题，为超大规模稀疏检索系统提供了可扩展的高效训练方案。实验证明该方法在显著提升GPU利用率和吞吐的同时，完全保持模型有效性，具备部署价值。

Abstract: State-of-the-art Learned Sparse Retrieval (LSR) models, such as Splade, typically employ a Language Modeling (LM) head to project latent hidden states into a lexically-anchored logit matrix. This intermediate matrix is subsequently transformed into a sparse lexical representation through element-wise operations (ReLU, Log1P) and max-pooling over the sequence dimension. Despite its effectiveness, the LM head creates a massive memory bottleneck due to the sheer size of the vocabulary (V), which can range from 30,000 to over 250,000 tokens in recent models. Materializing this matrix creates a significant memory bottleneck, limiting model scaling. The resulting I/O overhead between operators further throttles throughput and runtime performance. In this paper, we propose Sparton, a fast memory-efficient Triton kernel tailored for the LM head in LSR models. Sparton utilizes a fused approach that integrates the tiled matrix multiplication, ReLU, Log1P, and max-reduction into a single GPU kernel. By performing an early online reduction directly on raw logit tiles, Sparton avoids materializing the full logit matrix in memory. Our experiments demonstrate that the Sparton kernel, in isolation, achieves up to a 4.8x speedup and an order-of-magnitude reduction in peak memory usage compared to PyTorch baselines. Integrated into Splade (|V| ~ 30k), Sparton enables a 33% larger batch size and 14% faster training with no effectiveness loss. On a multilingual backbone (|V| ~ 250k), these gains jump to a 26x larger batch size and 2.5x faster training.

</details>


### [113] [Hyena Operator for Fast Sequential Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25027)
*Jiahao Liu,Lin Li,Zhiyuan Li,Kaixi Hu,Kaize Shi,Jingling Yuan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出HyenaRec，一种结合勒让德正交多项式核参数化和门控卷积的序列推荐模型，以线性复杂度在长序列场景下超越注意力基线，实现高达6倍训练加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于注意力的序列推荐模型存在二次复杂度问题，难以处理长用户历史；Hyena等次二次算子虽在语言建模中高效，但在推荐任务上因稀疏长序列的表征能力有限而潜力未被充分挖掘。

Method: 设计基于勒让德正交多项式的卷积核参数化来建模长期时序依赖，配合门控机制捕捉短期行为爆发，构建混合架构以平衡全局时序演化与局部用户兴趣，实现线性序列长度扩展。

Result: 在多个真实数据集上，HyenaRec在排序准确率上持续优于注意力、循环及其他基线模型，训练速度提升高达6倍，在长序列场景中效率优势尤为显著且不牺牲精度。

Conclusion: 多项式核参数化为序列推荐提供了一种原则性且可扩展的注意力替代方案，兼具高效率与强表征能力。

Abstract: Sequential recommendation models, particularly those based on attention, achieve strong accuracy but incur quadratic complexity, making long user histories prohibitively expensive. Sub-quadratic operators such as Hyena provide efficient alternatives in language modeling, but their potential in recommendation remains underexplored. We argue that Hyena faces challenges in recommendation due to limited representation capacity on sparse, long user sequences. To address these challenges, we propose HyenaRec, a novel sequential recommender that integrates polynomial-based kernel parameterization with gated convolutions. Specifically, we design convolutional kernels using Legendre orthogonal polynomials, which provides a smooth and compact basis for modeling long-term temporal dependencies. A complementary gating mechanism captures fine-grained short-term behavioral bursts, yielding a hybrid architecture that balances global temporal evolution with localized user interests under sparse feedback. This construction enhances expressiveness while scaling linearly with sequence length. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world datasets demonstrate that HyenaRec consistently outperforms Attention-, Recurrent-, and other baselines in ranking accuracy. Moreover, it trains significantly faster (up to 6x speedup), with particularly pronounced advantages on long-sequence scenarios where efficiency is maintained without sacrificing accuracy. These results highlight polynomial-based kernel parameterization as a principled and scalable alternative to attention for sequential recommendation.

</details>


### [114] [AuthorityBench: Benchmarking LLM Authority Perception for Reliable Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25092)
*Zhihui Yao,Hengran Zhang,Keping Bi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出 AuthorityBench 基准测试，用于评估大语言模型的信息权威性感知能力。通过在三个数据集（DomainAuth、EntityAuth、RAGAuth）上测试五种大语言模型，发现 ListJudge 方法在成本效益和性能上表现最佳，且基于权威性过滤可显著提升检索增强生成的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG 虽然能增强大语言模型的知识获取，但容易受到低权威来源的误导而传播虚假信息。当前研究尚未充分探索大语言模型是否能感知信息权威性这一超越语义理解的能力，缺乏系统性的评估基准，这限制了构建可靠知识检索系统的可能性。

Method: 1) 构建 AuthorityBench 基准，包含三个数据集：DomainAuth（1万网页域名，基于PageRank的权威性标注）、EntityAuth（2.2万实体，基于流行度的权威性标注）和 RAGAuth（120个查询及不同权威性的文档，用于下游任务评估）；2) 评估五种大语言模型在三种评判方法（PointJudge、PairJudge、ListJudge）和多种输出格式下的表现；3) 在RAG场景中验证权威性引导过滤的效果。

Result: 1) ListJudge 和 PairJudge 配合 PointScore 输出与真实权威性标签的相关性最强，其中 ListJudge 兼具最优的成本效益；2) 加入网页文本内容反而持续降低判断性能，表明权威性与文本风格是不同维度的概念；3) 在下游 RAG 实验中，基于权威性过滤大幅提升了答案准确性，证明了权威性感知对可靠知识检索的实际价值。

Conclusion: 大语言模型具备感知信息权威性的潜力，但需要专门的评估方法和优化策略。该研究验证了权威性感知在提升 RAG 系统可靠性方面的重要作用，为构建更 trustworthy 的信息访问系统提供了基础框架和实践指导。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances Large Language Models (LLMs) with external knowledge but remains vulnerable to low-authority sources that can propagate misinformation. We investigate whether LLMs can perceive information authority - a capability extending beyond semantic understanding. To address this, we introduce AuthorityBench, a comprehensive benchmark for evaluating LLM authority perception comprising three datasets: DomainAuth (10K web domains with PageRank-based authority), EntityAuth (22K entities with popularity-based authority), and RAGAuth (120 queries with documents of varying authority for downstream evaluation). We evaluate five LLMs using three judging methods (PointJudge, PairJudge, ListJudge) across multiple output formats. Results show that ListJudge and PairJudge with PointScore output achieve the strongest correlation with ground-truth authority, while ListJudge offers optimal cost-effectiveness. Notably, incorporating webpage text consistently degrades judgment performance, suggesting authority is distinct from textual style. Downstream experiments on RAG demonstrate that authority-guided filtering largely improves answer accuracy, validating the practical importance of authority perception for reliable knowledge retrieval. Code and benchmark are available at: https://github.com/Trustworthy-Information-Access/AuthorityBench.

</details>


### [115] [MCLMR: A Model-Agnostic Causal Learning Framework for Multi-Behavior Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25126)
*Ranxu Zhang,Junjie Meng,Ying Sun,Ziqi Xu,Bing Yin,Hao Li,Yanyong Zhang,Chao Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出MCLMR，一个基于因果学习的多行为推荐框架。通过构建因果图建模混杂效应并进行干预，使用混合专家自适应聚合辅助行为信息，并采用偏置感知对比学习对齐跨行为表示，在三个真实数据集上显著优于现有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统单行为推荐存在数据稀疏问题，现有多行为推荐方法缺乏建模用户行为习惯和商品多行为分布混杂效应的原则性框架，难以有效聚合异构辅助行为，也无法在语义鸿沟下对齐行为表示并消除偏置。

Method: 提出MCLMR模型无关因果学习框架：1)构建因果图建模混杂效应并进行干预以估计无偏偏好；2)采用基于混合专家的自适应聚合模块动态融合辅助行为信息；3)设计偏置感知对比学习模块以偏置感知方式对齐跨行为表示。

Result: 在三个真实世界数据集上的广泛实验表明，MCLMR在各种基线模型上均实现了显著的性能提升，验证了其有效性和通用性。

Conclusion: MCLMR框架有效解决了多行为推荐中的混杂效应和偏置问题，具有模型无关性和良好的泛化能力，为多行为推荐提供了新的因果推断视角。

Abstract: Multi-Behavior Recommendation (MBR) leverages multiple user interaction types (e.g., views, clicks, purchases) to enrich preference modeling and alleviate data sparsity issues in traditional single-behavior approaches. However, existing MBR methods face fundamental challenges: they lack principled frameworks to model complex confounding effects from user behavioral habits and item multi-behavior distributions, struggle with effective aggregation of heterogeneous auxiliary behaviors, and fail to align behavioral representations across semantic gaps while accounting for bias distortions. To address these limitations, we propose MCLMR, a novel model-agnostic causal learning framework that can be seamlessly integrated into various MBR architectures. MCLMR first constructs a causal graph to model confounding effects and performs interventions for unbiased preference estimation. Under this causal framework, it employs an Adaptive Aggregation module based on Mixture-of-Experts to dynamically fuse auxiliary behavior information and a Bias-aware Contrastive Learning module to align cross-behavior representations in a bias-aware manner. Extensive experiments on three real-world datasets demonstrate that MCLMR achieves significant performance improvements across various baseline models, validating its effectiveness and generality. All data and code will be made publicly available. For anonymous review, our code is available at the following the link: https://github.com/gitrxh/MCLMR.

</details>


### [116] [ColBERT-Att: Late-Interaction Meets Attention for Enhanced Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25248)
*Raj Nath Patel,Sourav Dutta*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出ColBERT-Att，在ColBERT晚期交互框架中显式引入注意力机制，通过利用查询与文档词项的注意力权重来建模相似度"重要性"，从而提升检索性能。实验在MS-MARCO、BEIR和LoTTE基准数据集上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ColBERT的晚期交互范式虽高效准确，但忽略了查询与文档词项间的注意力权重。这些权重能直观捕获相似度的重要性差异，对理解查询与文档相关性至关重要。缺乏注意力建模可能限制相关性判定的深度。

Method: 提出ColBERT-Att，将注意力机制显式集成到晚期交互框架中。该方法利用预训练语言模型的注意力权重，为查询与文档词元间的相似度计算赋予重要性权重，从而更精确地建模相关性。

Result: 在MS-MARCO、BEIR和LoTTE基准数据集上的实证评估表明，ColBERT-Att在所有数据集上均实现了召回准确率的显著提升，验证了注意力机制的有效性。

Conclusion: 在晚期交互框架中显式集成注意力机制能够显著提升神经信息检索性能，为利用注意力权重增强相关性建模提供了有效方案，证明了注意力机制在晚期交互范式中的重要价值。

Abstract: Vector embeddings from pre-trained language models form a core component in Neural Information Retrieval systems across a multitude of knowledge extraction tasks. The paradigm of late interaction, introduced in ColBERT, demonstrates high accuracy along with runtime efficiency. However, the current formulation fails to take into account the attention weights of query and document terms, which intuitively capture the "importance" of similarities between them, that might lead to a better understanding of relevance between the queries and documents. This work proposes ColBERT-Att, to explicitly integrate attention mechanism into the late interaction framework for enhanced retrieval performance. Empirical evaluation of ColBERT-Att depicts improvements in recall accuracy on MS-MARCO as well as on a wide range of BEIR and LoTTE benchmark datasets.

</details>


### [117] [Supercharging Federated Intelligence Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25374)
*Dimitris Stripelis,Patrick Foley,Mohammad Naseri,William Lindskog-Münzing,Chong Shen Ng,Daniel Janes Beutel,Nicholas D. Lane*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对私有数据孤岛间的知识分布问题，提出基于Flower的安全联邦RAG系统，实现本地检索与可信执行环境中的服务器端聚合生成，支持在不可信服务器场景下的保密远程LLM推理，并引入级联推理机制整合第三方模型作为辅助上下文而不泄露机密。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG假设文档集中访问，但实际应用中知识往往分布在私有数据孤岛中，集中化访问会破坏数据隐私性。同时，在存在诚实但好奇或已 compromised 服务器的场景下，如何实现保密的远程大语言模型推理是一个挑战。

Method: 提出基于Flower框架的联邦RAG系统，采用本地数据孤岛检索、服务器端在可信执行环境中进行聚合和文本生成的架构。创新性地引入级联推理机制，在保持机密性的前提下整合非保密的第三方模型（如Amazon Nova）作为辅助上下文。

Result: 该系统能够在数据分布在多个私有孤岛的情况下，实现保密的远程LLM推理，即使服务器是诚实但好奇的或已被 compromised，也能保护数据隐私。级联推理方法在不削弱保密性的同时，利用外部模型增强上下文信息。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了安全联邦RAG系统，解决了分布式私有数据场景下的知识检索与隐私保护矛盾，为数据孤岛间的保密AI推理提供了可行方案，并通过级联推理扩展了系统能力边界。

Abstract: RAG typically assumes centralized access to documents, which breaks down when knowledge is distributed across private data silos. We propose a secure Federated RAG system built using Flower that performs local silo retrieval, while server-side aggregation and text generation run inside an attested, confidential compute environment, enabling confidential remote LLM inference even in the presence of honest-but-curious or compromised servers. We also propose a cascading inference approach that incorporates a non-confidential third-party model (e.g., Amazon Nova) as auxiliary context without weakening confidentiality.

</details>
